Lower matrix LR regressed (`0.993758`), so I’m discarding it and restoring the best settings.

Optimizer LR changes did not help. A more structural training-loop knob is batch size: current total batch is `524288` tokens with two microbatches per optimizer step; I’ll try `262144` so each microbatch becomes an optimizer step, giving about twice as many updates in the same token budget.

The batch-size experiment is a single config change. I’m committing and running it.
